## ZIMAllRoomLeftResult

Callback for the results of leaving all rooms.

### Properties

  name="roomIDs"
  prototype="roomIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMAllRoomLeftResult"
  parent_type="class">
Room IDs.
</ParamField>

ANS Parameter

**Details**

Includes noise suppression mode.

  parent_type="class">

</ParamField>

## ZIMAudioError

**Details**

It can be used to record the error type and error information generated by the SDK, check the error code table on the ZEGO official website, and seek assistance from ZEGO technical support.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="code"
  prototype="code: ZIMAudioErrorCode "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioError"
  parent_type="class">
Error code.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="message"
  prototype="message: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioError"
  parent_type="class">
It can be used to record the error type and error information generated by the SDK, check the error code table on the ZEGO official website, and seek assistance from ZEGO technical support.
</ParamField>

The number of audio channels.
</ParamField>

## ZIMAudioMessage

Audio message object.

**Details**

Identifies the basic parameters of a message.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: If the Type parameter of the base class is Audio during callback, you can force the base class message object to be of this type.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="audioDuration"
  prototype="audioDuration: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required by the sender, if not filled, the audio message will fail to be sent When sending local audio messages.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileUID"
  prototype="fileUID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The unique ID of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageID"
  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The unique ID that identifies this message.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Can be used to index other messages.
- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="timestamp"
  prototype="timestamp: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the sending time of a message

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Used to present the sending time of a message, and can be used for message sorting.
- **Caution**: This is a standard UNIX timestamp, in milliseconds.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserID"
  prototype="senderUserID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Displays the userID of the sender of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationID"
  prototype="conversationID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessage"
  parent_type="class">

## ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo

Audio message lite info object.

**Details**

Identifies the basic parameters of a audio message.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="audioDuration"
  prototype="audioDuration: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required by the sender, if not filled, the audio message will fail to be sent When sending local audio messages.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>

## ZIMAudioPlayConfig

Audio Playback Configuration

**Details**

Playing configuration. Configuration specifies the audio file path and routing type that currently need to be played.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="filePath"
  prototype="filePath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioPlayConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The absolute path of the file needs to be played. Currently, only full absolute paths with the suffix .mp3 or .m4a are supported. When passing in file paths in other formats, the SDK will throw an illegal file path error.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="routeType"
  prototype="routeType: [ZIMAudioRouteType](./enum#zimaudioroutetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioPlayConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Starting audio routing type when playing.
</ParamField>

## ZIMAudioRecordConfig

Audio Recording Configuration

**Details**

Configure the recording file output path and maximum recording time during recording.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="filePath"
  prototype="filePath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioRecordConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The output path of the recording file. Currently, only full absolute paths with the suffix .mp3 or .m4a are supported. When passing in file paths in other formats, the SDK will throw an illegal file path error.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="maxDuration"
  prototype="maxDuration: number "
  parent_name="ZIMAudioRecordConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The maximum recording time, the default is 60000 ms, which is 60s. The unit of this parameter is milliseconds, and the maximum value does not exceed 300000.
</ParamField>

## ZIMCallInviteConfig

The behavior property of the Send Call Invitation setting.

**Details**

The behavior property of the Send Call Invitation setting.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="timeout"
  prototype="timeout: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCallInviteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The timeout setting of the call invitation, the unit is seconds. The range is  [1, 600].

<Note title="">
- **Required**: not required.
    
Default: 90.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="extendedData"
  prototype="extendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCallInviteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Extended field, through which the inviter can carry information to the invitee.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="pushConfig"
  prototype="pushConfig: [ZIMPushConfig](#zimpushconfig) "
  parent_name="ZIMCallInviteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Offline push configuration.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: not required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="mode"
  prototype="mode: [ZIMCallInvitationMode](./enum#zimcallinvitationmode) "
  parent_name="ZIMCallInviteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Call invitation mode configuration.
Supported Version: 2.9.0 or later.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: required.
default：GENERAL
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="enableNotReceivedCheck"
  prototype="enableNotReceivedCheck: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMCallInviteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
If the pass value is true, the system checks whether the call invitation is delivered in this call and subsequent calls.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: After the calling party sends a call invitation, if the called party does not receive the invitation within 5 seconds (3 or 4 seconds can be configured for technical support) because the user is disconnected or not online, the user status changes to notYetReceived. You can use this state flow to indicate to the user that the user may not be online. If the called party goes online before the call times out, the status changes to received received.
- **Required**: This is not required.
- **Default value**: false
- **Recommended value**: This property takes effect in version 2.15.0 and later, when the new version sends an invitation to a call with delivery detection turned on to the old version, which will continue to display the inviting status instead of notYetReceived.
</Note>
</ParamField>

- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.

- **When to call**: This callback is triggered when a developer invokes the [queryCombineMessageDetail] interface.
- **Caution**: Use [queryCombineMessageDetail] to pull the details of the combine message, and the success of the pull will be notified through this callback.
</Note>

- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@Everyone" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="mentionedUserIDs"
  prototype="mentionedUserIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMCommandMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@User".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in sending messages.
- **Required**: No.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@User" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageSeq"

## ZIMConversationFilterOption

Search filters related to the conversation.

**Details**

Configurable filter options when querying conversation list.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="marks"
  prototype="marks: std::vector\<int> "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationFilterOption"
  parent_type="class">
Conversation marks. Only integers in the range [1, 20] are supported. If the list contains -1, the query result will be all marked conversation; if the list contains 0, the query result will be all unmarked conversations; if multiple markers are passed, the query result will be the union of all passed markers; if the list is empty, the query result will be all conversations.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: This filter can be used when needing to search for conversations that include specified conversation marks.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationTypes"
  prototype="conversationTypes: std::vector<[ZIMConversationType](./enum#zimconversationtype)> "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationFilterOption"
  parent_type="class">
Conversation types. Only support one-on-one and group conversations.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When you need to search by conversation type, you can use this filter.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isOnlyUnreadConversation"
  prototype="isOnlyUnreadConversation: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationFilterOption"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to only query conversations with unread counts. Pass true to only query conversations with unread counts. Pass false to query without considering whether conversations have unread counts.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: It is necessary to query conversations that have a message unread count.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMConversationMessageReceiptReadSentResult

Callback interface for setting the read receipt conversation.

**Details**

Supported version: 2.5.0 and above.

Detailed description: Set the callback interface for the read receipt conversation.

Business scenario: Developers can judge whether the sending is successful through [errorCode] in the callback.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [sendConversationMessageReceiptRead] interface, this callback will be triggered.

Relevant interface: The success or failure of the conversation read result set by [sendConversationMessageReceiptRead] will be notified through this callback.

## ZIMConversationSearchConfig

Conversation search configuration.

**Details**

Conversation search configuration.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype=" nextFlag: number "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Pagination token, fill in 0 initially, and then fill in the nextFlag returned from the callback to retrieve data for the next page.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="totalConversationCount"
  prototype=" totalConversationCount: number "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of messages that can be retrieved in one search. It is recommended to be less than 20 to reduce performance overhead.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationMessageCount"
  prototype=" conversationMessageCount: number "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of local messages that can be retrieved for a single conversation in one search. It is recommended to be less than 10 to reduce performance overhead.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="keywords"
  prototype=" keywords: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Search keywords, supports up to 5. Otherwise, an error will occur. For example, if you pass in "1" and "2", the search results will only display conversations that contain both "1" and "2" keywords in the messages.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageTypes"
  prototype=" messageTypes: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Message types, can be used to specify message types. Support passing in multiple types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subMessageTypes"
  prototype=" subMessageTypes: number[] "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The subtypes of custom messages have a value range of [0,200]. Developers can use this range to search for specific custom types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserIDs"
  prototype=" senderUserIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Send user ID, supports up to 5. For example, if you pass in "zego2023", the search results will only display conversations where messages have been sent by the user "zego2023".
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="startTime"
  prototype=" startTime: number "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The starting point of the search, in milliseconds, with a default value of 0. The format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="endTime"
  prototype=" endTime: number "
  parent_name="ZIMConversationSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The ending point of the search, which must be greater than the startTime, in milliseconds. The default value is 0 and the format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>

## ZIMCustomMessage

Custom message object.

**Details**

Identifies a custom message.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: When calling back, if the Type parameter of the base class is Custom, the base class message object can be forcibly converted to this class.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.8.0 and above.
</Warning>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="message"
  prototype="message: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The text content of the message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subType"
  prototype="subType: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The subtype of the message, which is used by customers to customize the usage of different custom messages.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: The sender is required, otherwise the message will fail to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="searchedContent"
  prototype="searchedContent: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Search fields for custom messages. Since you cannot search for a custom message by directly searching the message field, you can concatenate the content you want to be searched in the custom message (such as the title of the poll, etc.) and put it in this parameter (the length is 64 bytes by default), so that follow-up search.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageID"
  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The unique ID that identifies this message.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Can be used to index other messages.
- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="timestamp"
  prototype="timestamp: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the sending time of a message

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Used to present the sending time of a message, and can be used for message sorting.
- **Caution**: This is a standard UNIX timestamp, in milliseconds.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserID"
  prototype="senderUserID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Displays the userID of the sender of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationID"
  prototype="conversationID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Conversation ID. Ids of the same conversation type are unique.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="direction"
  prototype="direction: [ZIMMessageDirection](./enum#zimmessagedirection) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Used to describe whether a message is sent or received.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="sentStatus"
  prototype="sentStatus: [ZIMMessageSentStatus](./enum#zimmessagesentstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Describes the sending status of a message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationType"
  prototype="conversationType: [ZIMConversationType](./enum#zimconversationtype) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The type of conversation to which the message belongs.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationSeq"
  prototype="conversationSeq: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Indicates the sequence number of the message in the conversation.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="orderKey"
  prototype="orderKey: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The larger the orderKey, the newer the message, and can be used for ordering messages.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="localMessageID"
  prototype="localMessageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
SDK locally generated MessageID, developers do not need to pay attention to.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isUserInserted"
  prototype="isUserInserted: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Describes whether the message is a message inserted by the developer through [insertMessageToLocalDB].
    
Default: false.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="receiptStatus"
  prototype="receiptStatus: [ZIMMessageReceiptStatus](./enum#zimmessagereceiptstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Describe the receipt status of the message

Business scenario: used to determine the status of the current message in the receipt message
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="extendedData"
  prototype="extendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
message extension field

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: You can add extended fields to the message and send it to the peer
- **Required**: no
- **Caution**: the length is 1k, you can contact technical support for configuration
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.6.0 or higher
</Warning>
</ParamField>

  name="localExtendedData"

  parent_type="class">
The expandable message field visible only on this end can store additional information locally, Through [updateMessageLocalExtendedData] change and currently has a length limit of 128K. If you have special requirements, please contact ZEGO technical support for configuration.

  name="isMentionAll"
  prototype="isMentionAll: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@Everyone".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in groups or rooms.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@Everyone" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in sending messages.
- **Required**: No.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@User" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>

## ZIMCustomMessageLiteInfo

Custom message lite info object.

**Details**

Identifies a custom message.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="message"
  prototype="message: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
The text content of the message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subType"
  prototype="subType: number "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
The subtype of the message, which is used by customers to customize the usage of different custom messages.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: The sender is required, otherwise the message will fail to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="searchedContent"
  prototype="searchedContent: string "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Search fields for custom messages. Since you cannot search for a custom message by directly searching the message field, you can concatenate the content you want to be searched in the custom message (such as the title of the poll, etc.) and put it in this parameter (the length is 64 bytes by default), so that follow-up search.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMCustomMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>

## ZIMErrorUserInfo

Error user information class.

### Properties

  name="userID"
  prototype="userID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMErrorUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User ID, a string with a maximum length of 32 bytes or less. It is customized by the developer. Only support numbers, English characters and '!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '(', ')', '+', '-', ':', ';', '&lt;', '=', '.', '&gt;', '?', '@', '[', ']', '^', '_', '\{', '\}', '|', '~'.

<ParamField
  name="userStatusUpdated"
  prototype="  userStatusUpdated(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), userStatusList: List<[ZIMUserStatus](#zimuserstatus)>): void"
  desc="User status change notification."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | zim instance. |
| userStatusList | List\<[ZIMUserStatus](#zimuserstatus)\> | A list with data about the user's online status. |

**Details**

User online status change notification.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: This callback can be used when you needs to pay attention to the online status of certain users, for example, the online group members need to be displayed. After subscribing to users through the subscribeUsersStatus method, the online status of the targeted users and the changes of their online status during the validity period of the subscription will be notified to you through this callback.
- **When to call /Trigger**: After the current user subscribes to the target user for the first time, the event will be triggered if the target user is added to the subscription list for the first time, or the subscribed user's online status or online platform list. In addition, the callback will also be triggered if the current user has opened a multi-terminal login and the online platform has changed.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.18.0
- **Restrictions**: When the userStatusUpdated callback returns the userStatus information of the current user, the onlineStatus will be unknown and the lastUpdateTime will be 0, which cannot truly present the online status. Map the online status of the current user according to connectionStateChanged.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="error"
  prototype="  error(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), errorInfo: [ZIMError](#zimerror)): void"
  desc="The callback for error information."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| errorInfo | [ZIMError](#zimerror) | Error information, please refer to the error codes document. |

**Details**

When an EXCEPTION occurs in the SDK, the callback prompts detailed exception information.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: It is recommended that developers listen for this callback notification and print the error information to the console during debugging after accessing the SDK, so that they can learn about the errors occurred during development and modify them in time.
- **When to call**: When an error occurs within the SDK, the SDK notifies the developer through this function callback.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 1.1.0 or above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="connectionStateChanged"
  prototype="  connectionStateChanged(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfConnectionStateChangedResult](#zimeventofconnectionstatechangedresult)): void"
  desc="The event callback when the connection state changes."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfConnectionStateChangedResult](#zimeventofconnectionstatechangedresult) | The result of the event callback. |

**Details**

When the connection status changes, the user will be notified of the current status and events through this callback.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: The [ZIMConnectionState] and [ZIMConnectionEvent] in this callback can be used to accomplish different business logic when you need to monitor the connection state and the events that cause the connection state to change.
- **When to call**: This function is called back when connection state changes.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 1.1.0 or above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="tokenWillExpire"
  prototype="  tokenWillExpire(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfTokenWillExpireResult](#zimeventoftokenwillexpireresult)): void"
  desc="A reminder callback that the token is about to expire."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfTokenWillExpireResult](#zimeventoftokenwillexpireresult) | The result of the event callback. |

**Details**

When receiving this callback, the developer should call the [renewToken] function to update the Token in time.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the authentication Token has only 30 seconds left, the SDK calls back this function to notify the developer to update the authentication Token. If the validity period of the authentication Token passed by the developer when [login] is less than 30 seconds, the authentication Token will be recalled after [login] is successful.
- **When to call**: For details, see authentication Token Generation https://doc-zh.zego.im/article/11617.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 1.1.0 or above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userInfoUpdated"

**Details**

In the multi-terminal login scenario, after the user modifies their information on device A, other online multi-terminal devices will receive this callback. For offline devices, after the user goes online, they need to call the [queryUsersInfo] interface to actively query user information.

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.11.0 or above.
</Warning>

- **When to call /Trigger**: After creating a ZIM instance through [create] and logging in.

<ParamField
  name="callUserStateChanged"
  prototype="  callUserStateChanged(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfCallUserStateChangedResult](#zimeventofcalluserstatechangedresult)): void"
  desc="Call the notification of the user status in the invitation invitation."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfCallUserStateChangedResult](#zimeventofcalluserstatechangedresult) | The result of the event callback. |

<Note title="">
- **When to call**: When a new member is invited to a call, or a member accepts, rejects, exits, or a member response times out, all users on the current call invitation whose status is "Inviting," "Accepted," and "Received" receive the callback here. If the member is not online at the time of notification, the call is still ongoing when the login succeeds. The status changes of all members during the offline period will be sent to the user at one time. 

 If the user is not the inviter who initiated this call invitation or is not online, the callback will not be received.
- **Related APIs**: [callInvite], [callingInvite], [callAccept], [callReject],[callQuit].
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="groupStateChanged"

**Details**

allback notification of group status change.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Scenarios that require interaction based on the group status.
- **When to call /Trigger**: A notification is triggered when a group is created, joined, left, or dismissed.
- **Related APIs**: [createGroup] : creates a group. [joinGroup] : joins a group. [leaveGroup], leave the group. [dismissGroup]; dismiss the group.
</Note>
</ParamField>

<ParamField
  name="conversationChanged"

**Details**

Trigger this callback to return notification of session updates when a session is added, deleted, modified, pinned or unpinned.

<Note title="">
- **When to call /Trigger**: Notifications are triggered when a new message is updated in the session, or when the session itself is added, deleted, or modified.
- **Caution**: ConversationID is the same as single chat toUserID and group chat GroupID.
- **Related APIs**: Triggered by [sendPeerMessage], [sendGroupMessage], [sendRoomMessage], [deleteConversation], [deleteMessage], [deleteMessageByConversationID], [updateConversationPinnedState].
</Note>

<ParamField
  name="groupMessageReceived"
  prototype="  groupMessageReceived(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfReceiveConversationMessageResult](#zimeventofreceiveconversationmessageresult)): void"
  desc="The callback for receiving group message."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfReceiveConversationMessageResult](#zimeventofreceiveconversationmessageresult) | The result of the event callback. |

**Details**

When the user is online, they can receive online group messages through this callback. Also, when the user logs back into the ZIM SDK, they can receive all the group chat messages received during the offline period (up to 7 days) through this callback.

Call timing: This callback occurs when a ZIM instance is created with [create] and a group member sends a message.

<Note title="">
- **Related callbacks**: You can send messages to other group members via [sendGroupMessage].
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.18.0  or above
</Warning>

**Details**

This callback is received when an in-room message is received.

Call timing: This callback occurs when a ZIM instance is created with [create] and a group member sends a message.

<Note title="">
- **Related callbacks**: You can send messages to other group members via  [sendRoomMessage].
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.0.0  or above
</Warning>

<Warning title="Deprecated">This method is deprecated in version 2.18.0, please use [roomMessageReceived] instead.</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageRepliedCountChanged"
  prototype="  messageRepliedCountChanged(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfMessageRepliedCountChangedResult](#zimeventofmessagerepliedcountchangedresult)): void"
  desc="Reply to the event that the number of message trees has changed."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">

**Details**

When there is a new reply message, the number of replies to the corresponding root message is notified through this event.

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.17.0  or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>

<ParamField
  name="roomMemberJoined"
  prototype="  roomMemberJoined(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfRoomMemberChangedResult](#zimeventofroommemberchangedresult)): void"
  desc="Callback when other members join the room."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfRoomMemberChangedResult](#zimeventofroommemberchangedresult) | The result of the event callback. |

**Details**

After joining a room, when other members also join this room, they will receive this callback.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When other members in the room join, this callback will be called.
- **When to call**:  After creating a ZIM instance through [create], and the user is in a room joined by other members, you can call this interface.
- **Caution**: If the user is not currently in this room, this callback will not be called.
- **Related APIs**: You can use [onRoomMemberLeft] to receive this callback when other room members leave.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 1.1.0 or above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="roomMemberLeft"
  prototype="  roomMemberLeft(zim: [ZIM](./class#zim), data: [ZIMEventOfRoomMemberChangedResult](#zimeventofroommemberchangedresult)): void"
  desc="Callback when other members leave the room."
  parent_name="ZIMEventHandler"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| zim | [ZIM](./class#zim) | ZIM instance. |
| data | [ZIMEventOfRoomMemberChangedResult](#zimeventofroommemberchangedresult) | The result of the event callback. |

**Details**

After joining a room, when other members leave the room, they will receive this callback.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When other members in the room leave the room, this callback will be called.
- **When to call**:  After creating a ZIM instance through [create], and the user is in the same room of other members, you can call this interface.
- **Caution**: If the user is not currently in this room, this callback will not be called.
- **Related APIs**: You can receive this callback when other room members join through [onRoomMemberJoined].
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 1.1.0 or above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>

## ZIMFileMessage

File message object.

**Details**

Identifies the basic parameters of a message.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: If the Type parameter of the base class is File during callback,
you can force the base class message object to be of this type.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileUID"
  prototype="fileUID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The unique ID of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">

  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMFileMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The unique ID that identifies this message.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Can be used to index other messages.
- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>

- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in groups or rooms.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.

</ParamField>

  name="conversationName"
  prototype="conversationName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
conversationName is the same as the groupName/userName value corresponding to the session.
</ParamField>

  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMConversationType](./enum#zimconversationtype) "

conversation type.

  parent_type="class">

</ParamField>

  name="lastMessage"
  prototype="lastMessage: [ZIMMessage](#zimmessage) "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
last message.
</ParamField>

  name="orderKey"
  prototype="orderKey: number "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
OrderKey is used to describe the order of messages in the session. The larger orderKey is, the newer it is.
</ParamField>

  name="notificationStatus"
  prototype="notificationStatus: [ZIMConversationNotificationStatus](./enum#zimconversationnotificationstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
session notification status.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationAvatarUrl"
  prototype="conversationAvatarUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Conversation avatar URL. The peer to peer chat conversation avatar URL is the same as the user avatar URL, and the group chat conversation avatar URL is the same as the group avatar URL.

Use Limit: the maximum number of characters is 500 bytes. There is no limit on special characters.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isPinned"
  prototype="isPinned: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
Whether the conversation is pinned.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="mentionedInfoList"
  prototype="mentionedInfoList: [ZIMMessageMentionedInfo](#zimmessagementionedinfo)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
When reminded in a message or reminded to everyone in a conversation, this array will record the reminders.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, you can display the number of reminders in the conversation list based on this array, and also display which user's reminder it is.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationAlias"
  prototype="conversationAlias: string "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
After the friend remarks are set through [updateFriendAlias], this parameter is changed for each chat conversation. After setting a group alias by [updateGroupAlias], the corresponding group chat conversation's parameter will be modified synchronously.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: After update alias for friends or groups, the corresponding conversation chooses to display the alias over the conversation name when rendering the conversation page.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="marks"
  prototype="marks: std::vector\<int> "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
Describes all the existing marks for the conversation.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: The business layer can group logic, etc., according to different conversations with different marks.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="draft"
  prototype="draft: string "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupConversation"
  parent_type="class">
Conversation draft, when draft set conversation will carry this parameter.
</ParamField>

groupID.

Required or not: Mandatory, it will be automatically generated in the background.

Value: Supports only digits, English characters, and '!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '(', ')', '+', '-', ':', ';', '&lt;', '=', '.', '&gt;', '?', '@', '[', ']', '^', '_', '\{', '\}', '|', '~'  and not by '#' at the beginning.

User name, defined by you. For version 2.0.0 and onwards, the string has a maximum length of 256 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userAvatarUrl"
  prototype="userAvatarUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMemberSimpleInfo"
  parent_type="class">
The user avatar, which is custom generated by the developer, is not restricted by special characters and has a maximum length of 500 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.13.0 and above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>

  prototype="userExtendedData: string "

Extended field information of the user.

## ZIMGroupMessageReceiptMemberListQueriedResult

Callback interface for querying the specific read/unread member list of group receipt messages.

**Details**

Supported version: 2.5.0 and above.

Detailed description: The callback interface for querying the specific read/unread member list of the group receipt message.

Business scenario: Developers can judge whether the sending is successful through [errorCode] in the callback.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [queryGroupMessageReceiptReadMemberList] / [queryGroupMessageReceiptUnreadMemberList] interface, this callback will be triggered.

### Properties

  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="nextFlag: number "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMessageReceiptMemberListQueriedResult"

</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userList"
  prototype="userList: [ZIMGroupMemberInfo](#zimgroupmemberinfo)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMessageReceiptMemberListQueriedResult"
  parent_type="class">

</ParamField>

## ZIMGroupMuteConfig

Group mute configuration.

**Details**

Group mute configuration.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: required.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="mode"
  prototype="mode: [ZIMGroupMuteMode](./enum#zimgroupmutemode) "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMuteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Group mute mode.

<Note title="">
- **Default value**: All.
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="duration"
  prototype="duration: number "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMuteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Group mute duration, the unit is seconds. The value is -1, which means permanent mute. If you need to implement non-permanent mute, the upper limit is 604800 (7 days). If you need to increase it, please contact ZEGO technical support.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="roles"
  prototype="roles: number[] "
  parent_name="ZIMGroupMuteConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Group role list.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: This field is only meaningful when ZIMGroupMuteMode is set to Custom.
- **Caution**: When there is a 3 (ordinary user) in the list, other roles must also be present and cannot be 1, 2, or 4. If only muting ordinary users is needed, ZIMGroupMuteMode should be set to Normal.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMImageMessage

Image message object.

**Details**

Identifies the basic parameters of a message.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: If the Type parameter of the base class is Image during callback,
you can force the base class message object to be of this type.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailLocalPath"
  prototype="thumbnailLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The thumbnail local path of the image file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailDownloadUrl"
  prototype="thumbnailDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Thumbnail external download URL of the image file. When developers upload thumbnails to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageLocalPath"
  prototype="largeImageLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageDownloadUrl"
  prototype="largeImageDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: large Image external download URL of the image file. When developers upload large Images to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="originalImageWidth"
  prototype="originalImageWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Original image width.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the original image,the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="originalImageHeight"
  prototype="originalImageHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Original image height.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the original image,the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageWidth"
  prototype="largeImageWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Large image width. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 720 pixels, with the other side being scaled proportionally. When the shortest side of the original image is less than 720 pixels, no compression is applied.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the large image, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageHeight"
  prototype="largeImageHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Large image height. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 720 pixels, with the other side being scaled proportionally. When the shortest side of the original image is less than 720 pixels, no compression is applied.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the large image, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailWidth"
  prototype="thumbnailWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Thumbnail width. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 198 pixels, with proportional scaling applied to the other side. If the shortest side of the original image is smaller than 198 pixels, no compression will be performed.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the thumbnail, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailHeight"
  prototype="thumbnailHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Thumbnail height. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 198 pixels, with proportional scaling applied to the other side. If the shortest side of the original image is smaller than 198 pixels, no compression will be performed.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the thumbnail, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>

  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>

  prototype="fileUID: string "

</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="sentStatus"
  prototype="sentStatus: [ZIMMessageSentStatus](./enum#zimmessagesentstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Describes the sending status of a message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationType"
  prototype="conversationType: [ZIMConversationType](./enum#zimconversationtype) "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The type of conversation to which the message belongs.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationSeq"
  prototype="conversationSeq: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Indicates the sequence number of the message in the conversation.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="orderKey"
  prototype="orderKey: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The larger the orderKey, the newer the message, and can be used for ordering messages.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="localMessageID"
  prototype="localMessageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
SDK locally generated MessageID, developers do not need to pay attention to.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isUserInserted"
  prototype="isUserInserted: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Describes whether the message is a message inserted by the developer through [insertMessageToLocalDB].
    
Default: false.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="receiptStatus"
  prototype="receiptStatus: [ZIMMessageReceiptStatus](./enum#zimmessagereceiptstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Describe the receipt status of the message

Business scenario: used to determine the status of the current message in the receipt message
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="extendedData"
  prototype="extendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
message extension field

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: You can add extended fields to the message and send it to the peer
- **Required**: no
- **Caution**: the length is 1k, you can contact technical support for configuration
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.6.0 or higher
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="localExtendedData"
  prototype="localExtendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The expandable message field visible only on this end can store additional information locally, Through [updateMessageLocalExtendedData] change and currently has a length limit of 128K. If you have special requirements, please contact ZEGO technical support for configuration.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isBroadcastMessage"
  prototype="isBroadcastMessage: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether the message is pushed by all employees.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Internal assignment.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isMentionAll"
  prototype="isMentionAll: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@Everyone".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in groups or rooms.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@Everyone" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="mentionedUserIDs"
  prototype="mentionedUserIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@User".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in sending messages.
- **Required**: No.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@User" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageSeq"
  prototype="messageSeq: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Indicates the sequence number of the message in the conversation.

## ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo

Image message lite info object.

**Details**

Identifies the basic parameters of a image message.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailLocalPath"
  prototype="thumbnailLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The thumbnail local path of the image file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailDownloadUrl"
  prototype="thumbnailDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Thumbnail external download URL of the image file. When developers upload thumbnails to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageLocalPath"
  prototype="largeImageLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The large image local path of the image file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageDownloadUrl"
  prototype="largeImageDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: large Image external download URL of the image file. When developers upload large Images to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="originalImageWidth"
  prototype="originalImageWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Original image width.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the original image,the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="originalImageHeight"
  prototype="originalImageHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Original image height.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the original image,the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageWidth"
  prototype="largeImageWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Large image width. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 720 pixels, with the other side being scaled proportionally. When the shortest side of the original image is less than 720 pixels, no compression is applied.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the large image, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="largeImageHeight"
  prototype="largeImageHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Large image height. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 720 pixels, with the other side being scaled proportionally. When the shortest side of the original image is less than 720 pixels, no compression is applied.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the large image, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailWidth"
  prototype="thumbnailWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Thumbnail width. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 198 pixels, with proportional scaling applied to the other side. If the shortest side of the original image is smaller than 198 pixels, no compression will be performed.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the thumbnail, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="thumbnailHeight"
  prototype="thumbnailHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Thumbnail height. When sending local images, the ZIM service will compress the shortest side of the original image to 198 pixels, with proportional scaling applied to the other side. If the shortest side of the original image is smaller than 198 pixels, no compression will be performed.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: When the user needs to draw the image UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the thumbnail, the unit is pixel.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMImageMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>

## ZIMLogConfig

Log configuration

**Details**

Configure the storage path of log files and the maximum log file size.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="logPath"
  prototype="logPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMLogConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The storage path of the log files. Refer to the official website document for the default path.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="logSize"
  prototype="logSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMLogConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The maximum log file size (Bytes). The default maximum size is 5MB (5 * 1024 * 1024 Bytes)
</ParamField>

## ZIMLoginConfig

Configuration of login-related parameters.

**Details**

Login-related parameters.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Used to set different parameters during login.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="userName"
  prototype="userName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMLoginConfig"
  parent_type="class">
User name.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Used in the scenario where user nickname is modified during login, leave it blank if no change is needed.
- **Required**: No.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="token"
  prototype="token: string "
  parent_name="ZIMLoginConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Token carried during login.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Only pass this parameter in the scenario where token is used for authentication.
- **Required**: No.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isOfflineLogin"
  prototype="isOfflineLogin: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMLoginConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Whether it is offline login.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Set this parameter to true when performing offline login.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="customStatus"
  prototype="customStatus: string "
  parent_name="ZIMLoginConfig"
  parent_type="class">
User-defined status, with a default maximum of 64 bytes and a default expiration time of 1 day. After expiration, it will be reset to an empty string. When logging in, if this field is an empty string (default is an empty string), the current user's custom status will not be modified.
</ParamField>

</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMMediaDownloadedResult

Callback for the result of downloading the file for the media message.

**Details**

Supported Versions: 2.1.0 and above.

Detail description: Callback for the result of downloading the file for the media message.

Business scenario: The developer can use the [errorCode] in the callback to determine whether the insertion is successful.

Notification timing: This callback is triggered when the developer calls the [downloadMediaFile] interface.

Related interfaces: Downloading the file for the media message through [downloadMediaFile], and the success will be notified through this callback.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="message"
  prototype="message: [ZIMMediaMessage](#zimmediamessage) "
  parent_name="ZIMMediaDownloadedResult"
  parent_type="class">
Message object.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMediaMessageSendNotification

The notification callback when the media message is sent, you can get the relevant information before the message object is sent through this notification

**Details**

Detailed description: Through this notification, developers can obtain relevant information before the message object is sent, such as localMessageID, etc.

Business scenario: When developers need to record and cache relevant information before sending a message, they can obtain it by listening to the notification.
    
 If no monitoring is required, it can be passed null.

### Methods
<ParamField
  name="onMessageAttached"
  prototype="  onMessageAttached(message: [ZIMMediaMessage](#zimmediamessage)): void"
  desc="The incoming message object is given a localMessgeID and returned."
  parent_name="ZIMMediaMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| message | [ZIMMediaMessage](#zimmediamessage) | The currently sent message object. |

**Details**

Supported version: 2.4.0 and above.

The incoming message object is given a localMessgeID and returned.

Service scenario: Before a message is successfully sent, it can correspond to its localMessageID to implement loading before sending.

Notification time: Triggered after the message is sent and before the message is successfully sent.
</ParamField>

Base class of message object

**Details**

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: Some of the parameters, such as Message ID, only have values ​​during the callback.
Developers do not need to assign values ​​to these parameters when they actively create this object for sending messages.
</Note>

This parameter only has a value during callback.

## ZIMMessageReactionUserQueryConfig

Configuration for querying reaction user list

**Details**

When querying reaction member, you need to configure this object.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="nextFlag: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReactionUserQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The flag of the paging query. For the first query, set this field to an empty string. If the "nextFlag" field of the [ZIMMessageReactionUserListQueriedCallback] callback is not an empty string, it needs to be set here to continue the query on the next page.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype="count: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReactionUserQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
How many members are retrieved in one query, 100 at most. Exceeding 100 will result in an error.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: To obtain members in pages to reduce overhead, it is recommended to obtain within 20 members at a time. If the value is 0, the SDK will query 100 members by default.
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="reactionType"
  prototype="reactionType: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReactionUserQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
reaction type, defined by you.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageReceiptInfo

receipt information.

**Details**

Detailed description: receipt information.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="status"
  prototype="status: [ZIMMessageReceiptStatus](./enum#zimmessagereceiptstatus) "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: receipt status.
</ParamField>

  name="messageID"
  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">

Business scenario: Developers can match the loaded message list according to this ID.
    
Is it required: No, SDK fills in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationID"
  prototype="conversationID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Session ID.

Business scenario: Receipt information used to indicate which session this belongs to.
    
Is it required: No, SDK fills in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="conversationType"
  prototype="conversationType: [ZIMConversationType](./enum#zimconversationtype) "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Session type.

Business scenario: Indicates the type of the session.

Is it required: If no, the SDK is filled.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="readMemberCount"
  prototype="readMemberCount: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: Indicates the number of people who have read the receipt.

Business scenario: When used to query receipt information, it can display how many people have read the message.
    
Is it required: no.
    
Default: 0.
    
 This value indicates how many people have read the message, it is only applicable to the message has been read; if the message is not sent by yourself, the value is 0.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="unreadMemberCount"
  prototype="unreadMemberCount: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: Indicates the number of unread people of the receipt.

Business scenario: When used to query receipt information, it can display how many people have unread the message.
    
Is it required: no.
    
Default: 0.
    
 This value indicates how many people have not read the message, and it is only applicable to the message that has been read; if the message is not sent by yourself, the value is 0.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isSelfOperated"
  prototype="isSelfOperated: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
In a multi-device login scenario, after device A sets the message receipt as read, other online multi-devices use it to distinguish whether the message receipt set by itself has been read.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="readTime"
  prototype="readTime: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Server-side timestamp when the message receipt was read.

<Note title="">
- **Default value**: 0.    
- **Caution**: For the sender, this value is the timestamp when all session members read the message. For the recipient, this value is the timestamp when the message receipt was set.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageReceiptsInfoQueriedResult

Callback interface for query receipt message read.

**Details**

Supported version: 2.5.0 and above.

Detailed description: Callback interface for querying receipt message information.

Business scenario: Developers can judge whether the sending is successful through [errorCode] in the callback.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [queryMessageReceiptsInfo] interface, this callback will be triggered.

Relevant interface: through [queryMessageReceiptsInfo], whether the result of querying the receipt information is successful or not will be notified through this callback.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="infos"
  prototype="infos: [ZIMMessageReceiptInfo](#zimmessagereceiptinfo)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptsInfoQueriedResult"
  parent_type="class">
Query receipt information.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="errorMessageIDs"
  prototype="errorMessageIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageReceiptsInfoQueriedResult"
  parent_type="class">
Query the wrong message ID of the message receipt information.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageReceiptsReadSentResult

Business scenario: Developers can judge whether the setting is successful through [errorCode] in the callback.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [sendMessageReceiptsRead] interface, this callback will be triggered.

Relevant interface: The success or failure of the message read result set by [sendMessageReceiptsRead] will be notified through this callback.

## ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig

Configuration for querying reply message list.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="nextFlag: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The flag of paginated query. When querying for the first time, set this field to 0. If the "nextFlag" field of the [queryMessageRepliedList] callback is not 0, it means that the query has not ended yet. You need to set it here to continue querying the next page.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype="count: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageRepliedListQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The number of queries per query. The upper limit is 100. Exceeding 100 will result in an error.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMMessageSearchConfig

Message search configuration.

**Details**

Message search configuration.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextMessage"
  prototype=" nextMessage: [ZIMMessage](#zimmessage) "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Paging fetch flag, which means fetching messages before or after nextMessage, with "before" or "after" determined by the order value. On the first search, nextMessage is null. On subsequent searches, nextMessage needs to pass in the last message in the message list queried last time.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype=" count: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
count It is recommended to keep the number of items less than 20 to reduce performance overhead.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="order"
  prototype=" order: [ZIMMessageOrder](./enum#zimmessageorder) "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
When the "order" is "DESCENDING" during message search, it means querying messages with sending time earlier than nextMessage. If it's the first message query (i.e. nextMessage is null), then query from the last message stored locally forward. When "order" is "ASCENDING", it means querying messages with sending time later than nextMessage. If it's the first message query (i.e. nextMessage is null), then query from the first message stored locally backward. The default is "DESCENDING".
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="keywords"
  prototype=" keywords: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Search keywords, up to 5 keywords are supported, otherwise an error will be reported. For example: passing in "1" and "2" will make the search results only show messages that contain both keywords "1" and "2".
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageTypes"
  prototype=" messageTypes: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Message types, can be used to specify message types. Support passing in multiple types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="subMessageTypes"
  prototype=" subMessageTypes: number[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The subtypes of custom messages have a value range of [0,200]. Developers can use this range to search for specific custom types.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserIDs"
  prototype=" senderUserIDs: string[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The user ID of the message sender, supporting up to 5 IDs. For example, if "zego2023" is passed in, the search results will only display all the messages sent by the user "zego2023" in that conversation.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="startTime"
  prototype=" startTime: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The starting point of the search, in milliseconds, with a default value of 0. The format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="endTime"
  prototype=" endTime: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSearchConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The ending point of the search, which must be greater than the startTime, in milliseconds. The default value is 0 and the format is UTC timestamp.
</ParamField>
