## ZIMMessageSendNotification

The notification callback when the message is sent, you can get the relevant information before the message object is sent through this notification

**Details**

Detailed description: Through this notification, developers can obtain relevant information before the message object is sent, such as localMessageID, etc.

Business scenario: When developers need to record and cache relevant information before sending a message, they can obtain it by listening to the notification.
    
 If no monitoring is required, it can be passed null.

### Methods
<ParamField
  name="onMediaUploadingProgress"
  prototype="  onMediaUploadingProgress(message: [ZIMMediaMessage](#zimmediamessage), currentFileSize: number, totalFileSize: number): void"
  desc="Progress callback for sending media messages."
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| message | [ZIMMediaMessage](#zimmediamessage) | The message object for the current file upload. |
| currentFileSize | number | The current progress, that is, the real-time size of the current file upload. |
| totalFileSize | number | Total progress, which is the total size of the current file. |

**Details**

Supported versions: 2.1.0 and above.

Detail description: The progress callback for sending media messages.

Business scenario: The developer can obtain the sending progress of the media message through this callback.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [sendMediaMessage] interface, the callback will be triggered, and will be triggered multiple times during the sending process.

Related interface: Through [sendMediaMessage], the sending progress will be notified through this callback.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="onMessageAttached"
  prototype="  onMessageAttached(message: [ZIMMessage](#zimmessage)): void"
  desc="The incoming message object is given a localMessgeID and returned."
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| message | [ZIMMessage](#zimmessage) | The currently sent message object. |

**Details**

Supported version: 2.4.0 and above.

The incoming message object is given a localMessgeID and returned.

Service scenario: Before a message is successfully sent, it can correspond to its localMessageID to implement loading before sending.

Notification time: Triggered after the message is sent and before the message is successfully sent.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="onMultipleMediaUploadingProgress"
  prototype="  onMultipleMediaUploadingProgress(message: [ZIMMultipleMessage](#zimmultiplemessage), currentFileSize: number, totalFileSize: number, messageInfoIndex: number, currentIndexFileSize: number, totalIndexFileSize: number): void"
  desc="Progress callback for sending multiple messages."
  parent_name="ZIMMessageSendNotification"
  parent_type="class">
**Parameters**

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| message | [ZIMMultipleMessage](#zimmultiplemessage) | The currently sent message object. |
| currentFileSize | number | The current total uploaded size. |
| totalFileSize | number | The total size of files to be uploaded. |
| messageInfoIndex | number | The index of the array where the currently uploaded file is located. |
| currentIndexFileSize | number | The uploaded size of the currently uploaded file. |
| totalIndexFileSize | number | The total size of the files currently being uploaded. |

**Details**

Supported versions: 2.19.0 and above.

Detail description: The progress callback for sending multiple messages.

Business scenario: Developers can use this callback to obtain the upload progress of the media files in the multiple  message.

Notification timing: When the developer calls the [sendMessage] interface, the callback will be triggered, and will be triggered multiple times during the sending process.

Related interface: Through [sendMessage], the sending progress will be notified through this callback.
</ParamField>

## ZIMMultipleMessage

Multiple message object.

**Details**

Detailed description: Identifies a multiple message.

 Only supports the multiple of text, image, file, audio, video, and custom messages, and the number of array does not exceed 20.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="messageInfoList"
  prototype="messageInfoList: [ZIMMessageLiteInfo](#zimmessageliteinfo)[] "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
It can contain text, image, file, audio, video, and custom messages. The array length does not exceed 20.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: It can be used to send text and image multiple messages.
- **Recommended value**: The total number of items does not exceed 20, the maximum number of image is 10, and the maximum number of file, audio, video and custom message is 1 each. The size and format restrictions of image, file, audio, and video are the same as those of the corresponding rich media messages.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageID"
  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The unique ID that identifies this message.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Can be used to index other messages.
- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="timestamp"
  prototype="timestamp: number "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the sending time of a message

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Used to present the sending time of a message, and can be used for message sorting.
- **Caution**: This is a standard UNIX timestamp, in milliseconds.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="senderUserID"
  prototype="senderUserID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Displays the userID of the sender of this message.
</ParamField>

  prototype="extendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
message extension field

<Note title="">

- **Required**: no
- **Caution**: the length is 1k, you can contact technical support for configuration
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.6.0 or higher
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="localExtendedData"
  prototype="localExtendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The expandable message field visible only on this end can store additional information locally, Through [updateMessageLocalExtendedData] change and currently has a length limit of 128K. If you have special requirements, please contact ZEGO technical support for configuration.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isBroadcastMessage"
  prototype="isBroadcastMessage: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether the message is pushed by all employees.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Internal assignment.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="isMentionAll"
  prototype="isMentionAll: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMMultipleMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@Everyone".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in groups or rooms.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@Everyone" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField

## ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate

Offline push private message template.

**Details**

According to [OPUSH DMS template check ability to access instructions] (https://open.oppomobile.com/documentation/page/info?id=12391), OPPO in new message classification on the basis of the new push DMS templates, After you have configured the private message template in the OPPO console, if you need to apply the corresponding template during push notifications, you can assign a value to the privateMessageTemplate in ZIMPushConfig.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="templateID"
  prototype="templateID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
The ID of the private message template pushed by OPPO must be carried when sending the corresponding private message template. If the category of OPPO in the resourceID is set to be classified as Content and Marketing, this field is invalid. Details please see [OPUSH DMS template check ability to access instructions] (https://open.oppomobile.com/documentation/page/info?id=12391
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="titleParameters"
  prototype="titleParameters: string "
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
json string, OPPO push title template filling parameters. For example, the private message template ID title template is: Welcome to $\{city\} $, $\{city\} $Welcome you. The content of this parameter is :" \{"city":" Beijing\}".
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="contentParameters"
  prototype="contentParameters: string "
  parent_name="ZIMOfflinePushPrivateMessageTemplate"
  parent_type="class">
json string, OPPO push content template filling parameter. Example: The content template corresponding to the private message template ID is: Welcome $\{userName\} $to $\{city\} $. The content of this parameter is :" \{"userName":" Tom ", "city":" Shenzhen City "\}.
</ParamField>

## ZIMRoomMemberAttributesListQueriedResult

Returns the query result of the user attribute list in the room.

**Details**

Supported version: 2.4.0.

Detail description: Returns the result of paging query of all user attribute lists in the room.
    
Business scenario: After querying room user attributes, the success or failure and query results can be known through this callback.
    
Notification timing: The result will be returned after the room user attribute query is completed.
    
Related interface: [queryRoomMemberAttributesList], query room user attributes.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="roomID"
  prototype="roomID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberAttributesListQueriedResult"
  parent_type="class">
Room ID.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="infos"
  prototype="infos: [ZIMRoomMemberAttributesInfo](#zimroommemberattributesinfo)[] "

## ZIMRoomMemberInfo

Room user information.

**Details**

Detail description: A class describing room user.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="userID"
  prototype="userID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User ID, a string with a maximum length of 32 bytes or less. It is customized by the developer. Only support numbers, English characters and  '!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '(', ')', '+', '-', ':', ';', '&lt;', '=', '.', '&gt;', '?', '@', '[', ']', '^', '_', '\{', '\}', '|', '~'.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userName"
  prototype="userName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User name, defined by you. For version 2.0.0 and onwards, the string has a maximum length of 256 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userAvatarUrl"
  prototype="userAvatarUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberInfo"
  parent_type="class">
The user avatar, which is custom generated by the developer, is not restricted by special characters and has a maximum length of 500 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.13.0 and above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userExtendedData"
  prototype="userExtendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Extended field information of the user.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: This property has a value only for room users.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMRoomMemberQueryConfig

Configuration for querying room member.

**Details**

When querying member, you need to configure this object.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="nextFlag"
  prototype="nextFlag: string "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The flag of the paging query. For the first query, set this field to an empty string. If the "nextFlag" field of the callback is not an empty string, it needs to be set here to continue the query on the next page.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="count"
  prototype="count: number "
  parent_name="ZIMRoomMemberQueryConfig"
  parent_type="class">
How many messages are retrieved in one query.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: To obtain messages in pages to reduce overhead, it is recommended to obtain within 100 messages at a time. If the value is 0, the SDK will query 100 room member by default.
- **Required**: Required.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMTextMessage

Normal text message object.

you can force the base class message object to be of this type.
</Note>

<Note title="">

- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>

  prototype="timestamp: number "

Whether to mention everyone. It can be presented as "@Everyone".

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: For example, it can be used in groups or rooms.
- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.
- **Caution**: This value does not add the "@Everyone" to the message text. Developers need to implement it themselves
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>
</ParamField>

- **Required**: No.

- **Available since**: 2.14.0 or above
</Warning>

</ParamField>

## ZIMUserFullInfo

User full information object.

**Details**

Identifies a unique user.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**:  that the userID must be unique under the same appID, otherwise mutual kicks out will occur.
It is strongly recommended that userID corresponds to the user ID of the business APP,
that is, a userID and a real user are fixed and unique, and should not be passed to the SDK in a random userID.
Because the unique and fixed userID allows ZEGO technicians to quickly locate online problems.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="baseInfo"
  prototype="baseInfo: [ZIMUserInfo](#zimuserinfo) "
  parent_name="ZIMUserFullInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User basic information.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userAvatarUrl"
  prototype="userAvatarUrl: string "
  suffixes={["deprecated"]}
  parent_name="ZIMUserFullInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: not required.

Use restrictions: The value is a maximum of 500 bytes and contains no special characters.
</Note>

<Warning title="Deprecated">Deprecated in version 2.13.0. To obtain the URL of a user's avatar, please refer to userAvatarUrl from the baseInfo.</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="extendedData"
  prototype="extendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMUserFullInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: not required.
    
Privacy Protection Statement: Do not pass in sensitive information involving personal privacy, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID numbers, passport numbers, real names, etc.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMUserInfo

User information object.

**Details**

Identifies a unique user.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**:  that the userID must be unique under the same appID, otherwise mutual kicks out will occur.
It is strongly recommended that userID corresponds to the user ID of the business APP,
that is, a userID and a real user are fixed and unique, and should not be passed to the SDK in a random userID.
Because the unique and fixed userID allows ZEGO technicians to quickly locate online problems.
</Note>

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="userID"
  prototype="userID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User ID, a string with a maximum length of 32 bytes or less. It is customized by the developer. Only support numbers, English characters and  '!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '(', ')', '+', '-', ':', ';', '&lt;', '=', '.', '&gt;', '?', '@', '[', ']', '^', '_', '\{', '\}', '|', '~'.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userName"
  prototype="userName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
User name, defined by you. For version 2.0.0 and onwards, the string has a maximum length of 256 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userAvatarUrl"
  prototype="userAvatarUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
The user avatar, which is custom generated by the developer, is not restricted by special characters and has a maximum length of 500 bytes.

<Note title="">
- **Required**: Not required.
- **Privacy reminder**: Please do not provide sensitive personal information, including but not limited to mobile phone numbers, ID card numbers, passport numbers, and real names.
</Note>

<Warning title="">
- **Available since**: 2.13.0 and above.
</Warning>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="userExtendedData"
  prototype="userExtendedData: string "
  parent_name="ZIMUserInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Extended field information of the user.

<Note title="">
- **Caution**: This property has a value only for room users.
</Note>
</ParamField>

## ZIMUserStatusSubscribeConfig

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: This field is required.
- **Value range**: ：1 to 43200 (30 days), and the unit is minute.
- **Caution**: After the subscription is expired, the subscribed user will be deleted from the subscription list, and the status changes of the user will not be synchronized to the subscriber.
</Note>
</ParamField>

<ParamField

<Note title="">

  name="videoFirstFrameLocalPath"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameDownloadUrl"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Video first frame external download URL of the video file. When developers upload thumbnails to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameWidth"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">

Business scenario: When the user needs to draw a picture UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the first frame of the video, the unit is pixel.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameHeight"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The height of the first frame of the video.

Business scenario: When the user needs to draw a picture UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the first frame of the video, the unit is pixel.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileUID"
  prototype="fileUID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The unique ID of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="messageID"
  prototype="messageID: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessage"
  parent_type="class">
The unique ID that identifies this message.

<Note title="">
- **Use cases**: Can be used to index other messages.
- **Caution**: When the developer actively creates a message, there is no need to modify this parameter.
This parameter only has a value during callback.
</Note>
</ParamField>

- **Caution**: This is a standard UNIX timestamp, in milliseconds.
</Note>

- **Required**: No.
- **Default value**: false.
- **Recommended value**: Set to true if you need to mention everyone.

## ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo

Video message lite info object.

**Details**

Identifies a video message.

Usage restrictions: Only supports video files with video encoding formats of H264 and H265. After the message is sent successfully, the width and height information of the first frame of the video can be obtained.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="videoDuration"
  prototype="videoDuration: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: Required by the sender, if not filled, the video message will fail to be sent when sending local video messages.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameLocalPath"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The video first frame local path of the video file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in it. After calling [downloadMediaFile] to download, the SDK will generate this value.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameDownloadUrl"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: Video first frame external download URL of the video file. When developers upload thumbnails to their own servers, the SDK can pass through this field to other users.

Required or not: optional on the sender side, this field will only take effect when fileDownloadUrl is filled in.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameWidth"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameWidth: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The width of the first frame of the video.

Business scenario: When the user needs to draw a picture UI, the parameter used to determine the width of the first frame of the video, the unit is pixel.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="videoFirstFrameHeight"
  prototype="videoFirstFrameHeight: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detailed description: The height of the first frame of the video.

Business scenario: When the user needs to draw a picture UI, the parameter used to determine the height of the first frame of the video, the unit is pixel.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileLocalPath"
  prototype="fileLocalPath: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
<Note title="">
- **Required**: If a local file is sent, this parameter must be set by the sender. Otherwise, the message fails to be sent.
</Note>
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileDownloadUrl"
  prototype="fileDownloadUrl: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The external download url of the media message is used for the developer to transparently transmit the media file to other users by filling in this URL when the developer uploads the media file to his own server.

Required or not: If an external URL is sent, this parameter is mandatory on the sender end.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileName"
  prototype="fileName: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The filename of the media file.

Required or not: If you are sending an external URL, you need to fill in this value and include the file extension. If a local file is sent, the value is optional.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="fileSize"
  prototype="fileSize: number "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Detail description: The size of the media file.

Required or not: The sender does not need to fill in, this value is generated by the SDK.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="type"
  prototype="type: [ZIMMessageType](./enum#zimmessagetype) "
  parent_name="ZIMVideoMessageLiteInfo"
  parent_type="class">
Identifies the type of this message.
</ParamField>

## ZIMVoIPConfig

Provides information about the iOS VoIP offline push.

**Details**

Provides information about the iOS VoIP offline push.

### Properties
<ParamField
  name="iOSVoIPHandleType"
  prototype="iOSVoIPHandleType: [ZIMCXHandleType](./enum#zimcxhandletype) "
  parent_name="ZIMVoIPConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The type of contact information for the VoIP caller, by default, is generic.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="iOSVoIPHandleValue"
  prototype="iOSVoIPHandleValue: string "
  parent_name="ZIMVoIPConfig"
  parent_type="class">
The contact information of the VoIP caller. It is related to iOSVoIPHandleType. When iOSVoIPHandleType is PhoneNumber, the Value is a sequence of digits; when iOSVoIPHandleType is EmailAddress, the Value is an email address; when the contact information is of other types, the Value typically follows some domain-specific format, such as a username, numeric ID, or URL.
</ParamField>
<ParamField
  name="iOSVoIPHasVideo"
  prototype="iOSVoIPHasVideo: boolean "
  parent_name="ZIMVoIPConfig"
  parent_type="class">
Video call or not. The default value is audio
</ParamField>

- **Default value**:  1.
